<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<UL>
<LI>Nature of work - Clinical Psychologist<BR></LI></UL>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>I&nbsp;process personal information to enable me to provide health services to&nbsp;my patients, to maintain&nbsp;my accounts and records which may include sensitive and personal information</P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<P>Types and classes of information processed:</P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<UL>
<LI>details of psychometric assessments 
<LI>notes of material covered in sessions 
<LI>personal details 
<LI>lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>family details 
<LI>goods and services 
<LI>financial details 
<LI>employment and education details</LI></UL>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<P>We also process sensitive information such as</P>
<UL>
<LI>&nbsp;physical and mental health details 
<LI>&nbsp;sexual life&nbsp; 
<LI>&nbsp;race and ethnic origin 
<LI>&nbsp;religious or other beliefs of a similar nature offences and alleged offences</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with:</P>
<UL>
<LI>healthcare professionals 
<LI>social and welfare organisations 
<LI>central government and other government office&nbsp; 
<LI>business associates 
<LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing 
<LI>suppliers and service providers; 
<LI>financial organisations 
<LI>current, past and prospective employers; </LI></UL>
<P>Who the information is processed about.</P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<P>I process information about</P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<UL>
<LI>patients 
<LI>customers and clients 
<LI>staff 
<LI>suppliers 
<LI>business cintacts 
<LI>professional advisers</FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana><BR></LI></UL>
<P>Transfers</B></P>
<P>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information is only shared within the European Economic Area (EEA). Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</P></FONT>

The sensitive types of information may include physical or mental health details, racial or ethnic origin and religious or other beliefs. This information is about survey respondents. <FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><STRONG>Nature of work - </STRONG></P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><STRONG>Community Energy Direct (CED) Nature of Work description <?xml:namespace prefix = o ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:office" /><o:p></o:p></STRONG></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt"><o:p><FONT face=Arial>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">CED is an industrial and provident society owned by its members, who are community interest bodies, with consumer-facing operations. <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">CED and its members are all bound by their constitutions to focus on achieving the following principles <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• delivering cost-effective energy; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• promoting the development and community ownership of low carbon energy <SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>generation assets; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• increasing community awareness of resource efficiency and sustainable development. <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">CED’s members are referred to below as Community Energy Societies. <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">CED’s activities include: <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to promote and encourage within the United Kingdom the formation and development of <I><STRONG>Community Energy Societies</STRONG></I>; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to promulgate principles, on which <I><STRONG>Community Energy Societies </STRONG></I>should operate and to issue guidance on best practice for <I><STRONG>Community Energy Societies </STRONG></I>in relation to financial management, accounting standards, corporate governance, openness, efficiency, democracy or any other aspect of the affairs of <I><STRONG>Community Energy Societies</STRONG></I>; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to comply with and monitor compliance by members with the Association’s principles; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to act as an association or representative body of <I><STRONG>Community Energy Societies </STRONG></I>in dealing with central, regional and local government, statutory bodies, regulators and such other bodies as the Association decides from time to time; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to act as a representative body for <I><STRONG>Community Energy Societies </STRONG></I>in order to negotiate commercial arrangements with third parties in the energy market <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to protect, promote and further the interests of <I><STRONG>Community Energy Societies</STRONG></I>; </SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN><SPAN style="COLOR: windowtext"><o:p><FONT size=3 face=Arial>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE: always; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to provide advice and services for payment or free of charge to <STRONG><I>Community </I><o:p></o:p></STRONG></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><I><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><STRONG>Energy Societies </STRONG></SPAN></I><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">in relation to any aspect of their affairs; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to assist in the resolution of disputes between Members; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• to consider draft rules submitted by an industrial and provident society applying for membership of the Association, and rule changes proposed by members in the light of the Association’s Principles and to exercise any power granted under the Rules of any <I><STRONG>Community Energy Society</STRONG></I>. <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">Practical examples of these activities, and how they may involve personal data are set out below:- <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• Introducing consumers either directly or indirectly (via its members) to switching services providers such as Which! <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• Running consumer energy switching schemes <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• Providing administrative support services for local smart-energy clubs, created by local community bodies such as housing associations and local authorities, whose aim is to attract consumers and encourage them to adopt energy efficient practices and participate in group energy-switching schemes <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• Surveying consumer attitudes to energy and energy usage <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• Creating and running websites as necessary to support the above actions <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=Default><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; COLOR: windowtext; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Calibri','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri">• CED is in partnership with the Department of Energy and Climate change (DECC), concerning elements of its work. All information shared with DECC as a result of CED’s work will be provided on an anonymised, aggregated basis.</SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana><P>Nature of work - Nursery School / Playgroup / After School Club</P> <P><Br></P> <P>Description of processing</P></B> <P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P><B><P>Nature of work - Nursery School / Playgroup / After School Club</P></B><P><Br></P><B><P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B> <P>We process personal information to enable us to provide childcare, encourage and supervise educational play, to advertise our services, to maintain our own accounts and records and to support and manage our staff.</P><P><Br></P><B> <P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B> <P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include: </P> <UL> <LI>personal details</LI> <LI>family details</LI> <LI>GP contact details</LI> <LI>lifestyle and social circumstances</LI> <LI>digital images of the childs progress</LI> <LI>financial details</LI> <LI>education and employment details</LI> <LI>goods or services provided</LI></UL><P><Br></P> <P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include: </P> <UL> <LI>physical or mental health details</LI> <LI>racial or ethnic origin</LI> <LI>religious or other beliefs</LI> <LI>trade union membership</LI></UL><P><Br></P><B><P>Who the information is processed about</P></B> <P>We process personal information about: </P> <UL> <LI>our employees</LI> <LI>the children in our care</LI> <LI>advisers, complainants, enquirers</LI> <LI>suppliers</LI></UL><P><Br></P><B> <P>Who the information may be shared with</P></B> <P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P><P><Br></P> <P>Where necessary or required we share information with: </P> <UL> <LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing</LI> <LI>healthcare, social and welfare advisers or practitioners</LI> <LI>business associates</LI> <LI>financial organisations and professional advisers</LI> <LI>credit reference agencies, debt collection and tracing agencies</LI> <LI>education, educators and examining bodies</LI> <LI>current, past or prospective employers</LI> <LI>employment and recruitment agencies</LI> <LI>schools</LI> <LI>local and central government</LI> <LI>persons making an enquiry or complaint</LI> <LI>suppliers</LI> <LI>service providers</LI></UL></FONT><P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>Consultancy and Advisory Services </B></P>
<P>Information is processed for consultancy and advisory services that are offered. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, financial details, and the goods and services provided. This information may be about customers and clients. Where necessary this information is shared with the data subject themselves, business associates and other professional advisers, current, past or prospective employers and service providers.</P></FONT><P><Br></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B> <P>Undertaking Research </P></B><P>Personal information is also processed in order to undertake research. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, lifestyle and social circumstances, financial details, good and services. The sensitive types of information may include physical or mental health details, racial or ethnic origin and religious or other beliefs. This information is about survey respondents. Where necessary or required this information may be shared with customers and clients, agents, service providers, survey and research organisations.</P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Transfers</B></P>
<P>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information is only shared within the European Economic Area (EEA). Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</P></FONT>

<LI>financial details

<LI>offences and alleged offences 
<LI>racial or ethnic origin 
<LI>religious or other beliefs of a similar nature</LI></UL><B>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about our customers, clients and employees, complainants and enquirers, suppliers, advisers and other professional experts.</P>

<P>Who the information may be shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with:</P>
<UL>
<LI>business associates and other professional advisers 
<LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing

<LI>current, past or prospective employers 
<LI>educators and examining bodies 
<LI>suppliers and services providers 
<LI>traders in personal data</LI></UL></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>

<LI>goods or services provided</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>physical or mental health details 
<LI>racial or ethnic origin 
<LI>religious or other beliefs of a similar nature </LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about our:</P>
<UL>
<LI>employees 
<LI>customers and clients 
<LI>suppliers and services providers 
<LI>advisers, consultants and other professional experts 
<LI>complainants and enquirers
<LI>relatives, guardians and associates of the data subject</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information may be shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with:</P>
<UL>
<LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing 
<LI>employment and recruitment agencies 
<LI>current, past and prospective employers 
<LI>educators and examining bodies 
<LI>central government 
<LI>credit reference agencies 
<LI>suppliers and service providers 
<LI>debt collection and tracing agencies 
<LI>financial organisations
<LI>ombudsmen and regulatory authorities 
<LI>healthcare social and welfare advisors and practitioners</LI></UL></FONT>
<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>Providing Financial Services and Advice</B></P>
<P>Personal information is also processed in order to provide financial services and advice. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, lifestyle and social circumstances, financial details, goods and services and sensitive classes of information that may include physical or mental health details. This information may be about clients, family and associates of clients, suppliers and enquirers. Where necessary or required this information is shared with the data subjects themselves, professional advisers and consultants, services providers, credit reference agencies.</P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P>

<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - General business </P>
<P></B></P><B>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P><B>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to promote our goods and services, to maintain our accounts and records and to support and manage our staff. </P>
<P>Our main objective is the reporting of offences under the Wildlife and Countryside Act and related legislation.</P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>goods or services provided
<LI>offenders and suspected offenders
<LI>obvious distinguishing marks/features for possible identification</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>racial or ethnic origin </LI></UL>
<P>We process personal information about our:</P>
<UL>
<LI>employees 
<LI>suppliers and services providers 
<LI>complainants and enquirers
<LI>offenders and suspected offenders</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information may be shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with:</P>
<UL>
<LI>suppliers and service providers 
<LI>local government
<LI>police forces
<LI>landowners
<LI>Natural England</LI></UL>
<P></FONT><STRONG><FONT size=2>&nbsp;Transfers</FONT></STRONG></P>
<P><FONT size=2 face=verdana>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information is only shared within the European Economic Area (EEA). Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</P></FONT>

<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana,Bold','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Verdana,Bold'"><STRONG><FONT face=verdana>CCTV - Crime Prevention and/or Staff Monitoring<?xml:namespace prefix = o ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:office" /><o:p></o:p></FONT></STRONG></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana"><FONT face=verdana>CCTV is used for maintaining the security of property and premises and for preventing and investigating crime, it may also be used to monitor staff when carrying out work duties. For these reasons the information processed may include visual images, personal appearance and behaviours. This information may be about staff, customers and clients, offenders and suspected offenders, members of the public and those inside, entering or in the immediate vicinity of the area under surveillance. Where necessary or required this information is shared with the data subjects themselves, employees and agents, services providers, police forces, security organisations and persons making an enquiry</FONT></SPAN></P></FONT></FONT>

<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">Who information may be shared with<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>

Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the data protection act. What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - Indoor Rock Climbing Centre</P></B>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to provide a service to our members, to promote our services, to maintain our own accounts and records and to support and manage our employees.</P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>family and associate details 
<LI>lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>employment and education details 
<LI>financial details 
<LI>membership details</LI></UL>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include:&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<UL>
<LI>physical or mental health details</LI></UL><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about:</P>
<UL>
<LI>members&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<LI>employees</LI></UL>
<P><B>Who the information may be shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with: </P>
<UL>
<LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal information we are processing </LI></UL></FONT>
<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - Healthcare</P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>

<LI>religious or other beliefs of a similar nature

<P>We process personal information about our:</P>
<UL>
<LI>patients 
<LI>customers and clients 
<LI>staff 
<LI>suppliers 
<LI>business contacts 
<LI>professional advisers</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>

<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>

<LI>social and welfare organisations 
<LI>central government

<LI>suppliers and service providers; 
<LI>financial organisations 
<LI>current, past and prospective employers; 
<LI>employment agencies and examining bodies</LI></UL></FONT>
<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>CCTV - Crime Prevention and/or Staff Monitoring </B></P>
<P>CCTV is used for maintaining the security of property and premises and for preventing and investigating crime, it may also be used to monitor staff when carrying out work duties. For these reasons the information processed may include visual images, personal appearance and behaviours. This information may be about staff, customers and clients, offenders and suspected offenders, members of the public and those inside, entering or in the immediate vicinity of the area under surveillance. Where necessary or required this information is shared with the data subjects themselves, employees and agents, services providers, police forces, security organisations and persons making an enquiry.</P></FONT>
<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>Undertaking Research </P></B>
<P>Personal information is also processed in order to undertake research. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, lifestyle and social circumstances, financial details, good and services. The sensitive types of information may include physical or mental health details, racial or ethnic origin and religious or other beliefs. This information is about survey respondents. Where necessary or required this information may be shared with customers and clients, agents, service providers, survey and research organisations.</P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P></B></FONT>
<B><FONT size=5>
<P><FONT size=2>Nature of work - Payment Scheme</FONT></P>
<P><FONT size=2></FONT>&nbsp;</P></FONT><FONT face=Verdana,Bold>
<P><FONT size=2>Description of processing</FONT></P></B></FONT><FONT size=2 face=Verdana>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information may be processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances.</P>
<P></FONT><B><FONT face=Verdana,Bold><FONT size=2></FONT></FONT></B>&nbsp;</P>
<P><B><FONT face=Verdana,Bold><FONT size=2>Reasons/purposes for processing information</FONT></P></B></FONT><FONT size=2 face=Verdana>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to provide payment services to the UK banking industry, including the making of electronic payments by financial institutions. We also process personal information to enable us to promote and advertise our services; manage and support our staff; and maintain our own accounts and records. We may also process personal information relating to the Bank of England’s Real Time Gross Settlement System for the purposes of preparing aggregate data and analysing risk in the UK payment and settlement systems. </P>
<P>&nbsp;</P></FONT><B><FONT face=Verdana,Bold>
<P><FONT size=2>Type/classes of information processed</FONT></P></B></FONT><FONT size=2 face=Verdana>
<P>With respect to providing payment services to the UK banking industry, we may also process data which includes:</P></FONT><FONT face=Symbol>
<UL>
<LI></FONT><FONT face=Verdana><FONT size=2>personal details</FONT></LI></FONT><FONT face=Symbol>
<LI></FONT><FONT face=Verdana><FONT size=2>family details</FONT></LI></FONT><FONT face=Symbol>
<LI></FONT><FONT face=Verdana><FONT size=2>financial details</FONT></LI></FONT><FONT face=Symbol>
<LI></FONT><FONT face=Verdana><FONT size=2>education and employment details</FONT></LI></FONT><FONT face=Symbol>
<LI></FONT><FONT face=Verdana><FONT size=2>goods and services provided</FONT></LI></FONT><FONT face=Symbol>
<LI></FONT><FONT face=Verdana><FONT size=2>lifestyle and social circumstances</FONT></LI></FONT><FONT face=Symbol>
<LI></FONT><FONT face=Verdana><FONT size=2>visual images, personal appearance and behaviour</FONT></LI></UL>
<P><FONT size=2>We may also process sensitive classes of information that may include:</FONT></P></FONT><FONT face=Symbol>
<UL>

<P>Nature of work - Unitary Authority</P></B>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Description of Processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a very broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation directly to ask about your personal circumstances. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to provide a range of government services to local people and businesses which include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>maintaining our own accounts and records 
<LI>supporting and managing our employees 
<LI>promoting the services we provide 
<LI>marketing our local tourism 
<LI>carrying out health and public awareness campaigns 
<LI>managing our property 
<LI>providing leisure and cultural services 
<LI>provision of education 
<LI>carrying out surveys 
<LI>administering the assessment and collection of taxes and other revenue including benefits and grants 
<LI>licensing and regulatory activities 
<LI>local fraud initiatives 
<LI>the provision of social services 
<LI>crime prevention and prosecution offenders including the use of CCTV 
<LI>corporate administration and all activities we are required to carry out as a data controller and public authority 
<LI>undertaking research 
<LI>the provision of all commercial services including the administration and enforcement of parking regulations and restrictions 
<LI>the provision of all non-commercial activities including refuse collections from residential properties, 
<LI>internal financial support and corporate functions 
<LI>managing archived records for historical and research reasons 
<LI>data matching under local and national fraud initiatives</LI></UL>

<P>We do not transfer any personal information outside the European Economic Area (EEA)</P></FONT>
<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - General business </P>
<P></B></P><B>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P><B>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to promote our goods and services, to maintain our accounts and records and to support and manage our staff. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>family, lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>financial details 
<LI>employment and education details 
<LI>goods or services provided</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>physical or mental health details 
<LI>racial or ethnic origin 
<LI>religious or other beliefs of a similar nature 
<LI>trade union membership</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about our:</P>
<UL>
<LI>employees 
<LI>customers and clients 
<LI>suppliers and services providers 
<LI>advisers, consultants and other professional experts 
<LI>complainants and enquirers</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information may be shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with:</P>
<UL>
<LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing 
<LI>employment and recruitment agencies 
<LI>current, past and prospective employers 
<LI>educators and examining bodies 
<LI>central government 
<LI>credit reference agencies 
<LI>suppliers and service providers 
<LI>debt collection and tracing agencies 
<LI>financial organisations</LI></UL></FONT>
<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>Consultancy and Advisory Services </B></P>
<P>Information is processed for consultancy and advisory services that are offered. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, financial details, and the goods and services provided. This information may be about customers and clients. Where necessary this information is shared with the data subject themselves, business associates and other professional advisers, current, past or prospective employers and service providers.</P></FONT>
<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>Undertaking Research </P></B>
<P>Personal information is also processed in order to undertake research. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, lifestyle and social circumstances, financial details, good and services. The sensitive types of information may include physical or mental health details, racial or ethnic origin and religious or other beliefs. This information is about survey respondents. Where necessary or required this information may be shared with customers and clients, agents, service providers, survey and research organisations.</P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>

<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 10pt" class=MsoNormal><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN style="LINE-HEIGHT: 115%; FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"></SPAN></B></FONT></FONT></B></B><SPAN style="LINE-HEIGHT: 115%; FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas.<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>When this is needed information may be transferred to countries or territories around the world.<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>We are required to ensure that when we need to do this we comply with the Data Protection Act.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></FONT>

<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2" class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore">·<SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">sexual life<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana,Bold','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Verdana,Bold'"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana,Bold','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Verdana,Bold'">Who the information is processed about<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">We process personal information about our staff, our customers and clients, our suppliers, our advisers and other professional experts, complainants, correspondents and enquirers, relatives, guardians and associates of our employees and our clients. <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana,Bold','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Verdana,Bold'"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana,Bold','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Verdana,Bold'">With whom the information may be shared<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations with whom we may need to share some of the personal information we process (for one or more reasons). Where necessary or required we share information with:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

<P><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-language: EN" lang=EN>Marketing and Communication<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-language: EN" lang=EN>To support our business, we also process personal data for the purposes of marketing and communications. The information processed may include name, contact details, family details, lifestyle and social circumstances, and financial details. We do not process sensitive information for marketing purposes. <SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-language: EN" lang=EN>This information may be about our staff and their family and associates,<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>our clients and their family and associates, members or supporters of our clients, suppliers to us or to our clients, and enquirers to us or our clients, our advisers, consultants, and other professional experts. <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with other organisations within our same company group. </SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-language: EN" lang=EN>When working with personal data for marketing purposes, we may contract with trusted partners to provide processing on our behalf. </SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">Where any of these occurs, we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA).<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana,Bold','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Verdana,Bold'"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana,Bold','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Verdana,Bold'">CCTV - Crime Prevention and/or Staff Monitoring</SPAN></B><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana,Bold','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Verdana,Bold'"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">CCTV is used for maintaining the security of property and premises and for preventing and investigating crime. It may also be used to monitor staff and suppliers when carrying out work duties. For these reasons the information processed may include visual images, personal appearance and behaviours. This information may be about staff, customers and clients, offenders and suspected offenders, members of the public and those inside, entering or in the immediate vicinity of the area under surveillance. Where necessary or required this information is shared with the data subjects themselves, employees and agents, services providers, police forces, security organisations and persons making an enquiry.</SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana"><o:p></o:p></SPAN>&nbsp;</P>
<P><B><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-language: EN" lang=EN>Consulting and Advisory Services<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>

To provide these services, we may process personal data including </SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; COLOR: black; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-language: EN" lang=EN>names, contact details, family details, lifestyle and social circumstances, financial details, education and training details, and employment details. We may also have reason to process sensitive personal data including trade union membership and physical or mental health or condition.</SPAN></P>

<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: normal; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Verdana">It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information may be transferred to countries or territories around the world. Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act. <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - Trustees of a Pension Scheme</P></B>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information as trustees of pension funds to enable us to administer a funded pension or superannuation scheme.</P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>family details 
<LI>goods and services 
<LI>lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>financial details 
<LI>employment details </LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include physical or mental health details.</P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about: </P>
<UL>
<LI>customers and clients 
<LI>trustees 
<LI>members and beneficiaries 
<LI>employers and employees of other organisations </LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information may be shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with: </P>
<UL>
<LI>claimants, beneficiaries, assignees and payees 
<LI>pension schemes with which the person whose personal information we are processing has an association 
<LI>trade and business associates and professional advisers 
<LI>healthcare, social and welfare organisations 
<LI>financial organisations and advisers 
<LI>central and local government 
<LI>service providers 
<LI>ombudsmen and regulatory authorities 
<LI>suppliers 
<LI>family, associates or representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing 
<LI>current, past or prospective employers</LI></UL></FONT><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA">Transfers</SPAN></P>
<P><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA"></SPAN>&nbsp;</P>

Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act</SPAN><BR></P>
<P><STRONG>Transfers</STRONG></P></FONT>
<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - Financial, Mortgage and Insurance Services</P></B>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P><B>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to act as an intermediary for any financial transactions including mortgage and insurance broking, and debt administration to our clients; promote our goods and services; maintain our own accounts and records and to support and manage our staff.</P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include: </P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>family details 
<LI>lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>financial details 
<LI>employment and education details 
<LI>goods or services provided</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include: </P>
<UL>
<LI>physical or mental health details 
<LI>racial or ethnic origin 
<LI>religious or other beliefs 
<LI>trade union membership 
<LI>offences and alleged offences</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about:</P>
<UL>
<LI>clients 
<LI>suppliers 
<LI>professional advisers and consultants 
<LI>enquirers, complainants 
<LI>employees</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information may be shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with: </P>
<UL>
<LI>current, past or prospective employers 
<LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing 
<LI>financial organisations 
<LI>business associates and professional advisers 
<LI>educators and examining bodies 
<LI>employment and recruitment agencies 
<LI>healthcare and welfare organisations 
<LI>credit reference agencies 
<LI>debt collection and tracing agencies 
<LI>other companies in the same group 
<LI>suppliers and services providers 
<LI>trade and employer associations 
<LI>central government 
<LI>law enforcement and prosecuting authorities 
<LI>ombudsmen and regulatory authorities 
<LI>traders in personal data 
<LI>courts and tribunals</LI></UL></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P>

<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - Charity (Local)</P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to provide a voluntary service for the benefit of the public in a particular geographical area as specified in our constitution; to provide education; administer membership records; to fundraise and promote the interests of the charity; manage our employees and volunteers; maintain our own accounts and records.</P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>family detail 
<LI>lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>membership details 
<LI>goods and services provided
<LI>financial details 
<LI>education and training details&nbsp;
<LI>employment details
<LI>trade union membership</LI></UL>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include: </P>
<UL>
<LI>physical or mental health details 
<LI>racial or ethnic origin 
<LI>religious or other beliefs of a similar nature
<LI>sexual life
<LI>offences (including alleged offences)
<LI>criminal proceedings, outcomes and sentences</LI></UL><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about:</P>
<UL>
<LI>members or supporters
<LI>staff including volunteers, agents, temporary and casual workers
<LI>customers and clients
<LI>relatives, guardians and associates of the data subject
<LI>suppliers
<LI>trustees 
<LI>complainants, correspondents and enquirers&nbsp;
<LI>enquirers 
<LI>advisers, consultants and other professional experts
<LI>students and pupils
<LI>offenders and suspected offenders</LI></UL>
<P><B>Who the information may be&nbsp;shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with:</P>
<UL>
<LI>data subjects themselves
<LI>members 
<LI>relatives, guardians or other persons associated with the data subject
<LI>employees 
<LI>current, past and prospective employers 
<LI>healthcare, social and welfare organisations 
<LI>education, training establishments&nbsp;and examining bodies 
<LI>financial organisations&nbsp;and advisers
<LI>credit reference agencies
<LI>traders in personal data
<LI>trader employer associations and professional bodies
<LI>police forces
<LI>employment and recruitment agencies 
<LI>survey or research organisations 
<LI>business associates and professional advisers 
<LI>employees and agents of the data controller
<LI>other companies in the same group as the data controller
<LI>suppliers, providers of goods and services 
<LI>local and central government 
<LI>persons making an enquiry or complaint
<LI>other voluntary and charitable organisations
<LI>ombudsmen and regulatory authorities
<LI>the media
<LI>data processors</LI></UL></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Transfers</B></P>
<P>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information is only shared within the European Economic Area (EEA). Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</P></FONT>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo4" class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore">·<SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'"><FONT size=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><FONT face=Arial>landlords<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p><FONT face=Arial>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=MsoNormal><B><SPAN style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><FONT face=Arial>Transferring information overseas<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><FONT face=Arial>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information may be transferred to countries or territories around the world. Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - Charity (National)</P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to provide a voluntary service for the benefit of the national public as specified in our constitution; administer membership records; to fundraise and promote the interests of the charity; manage our employees and volunteers; maintain our own accounts and records.</P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>family details 
<LI>lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>membership details 
<LI>goods and services 
<LI>financial details 
<LI>education and employment details </LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include: </P>
<UL>
<LI>physical or mental health details 
<LI>racial or ethnic origin 
<LI>religious or other beliefs of a similar nature 
<LI>offences and alleged offences 
<LI>criminal proceedings, outcomes and sentences 
<LI>trade union membership</LI></UL><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about: </P>
<UL>
<LI>members 
<LI>staff, volunteers 
<LI>supporters 
<LI>complainants, enquirers 
<LI>advisers 
<LI>representatives of other organisations </LI></UL>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with: </P>
<UL>
<LI>members 
<LI>family, associates or representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing 
<LI>employees 
<LI>current, past and prospective employers 
<LI>healthcare, social and welfare organisations 
<LI>providers of goods and services 
<LI>educator and examining bodies 
<LI>financial organisations 
<LI>employment and recruitment agencies 
<LI>survey and research organisations 
<LI>business associates and professional advisers 
<LI>police forces 
<LI>local and central government 
<LI>other companies in the same group as the data controller 
<LI>other voluntary and charitable organisations</LI></UL></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Transfers</B></P>
<P>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information is only shared within the European Economic Area (EEA). Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</P></FONT>
<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>

<P><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">TRANSFERS</SPAN></P>
<P><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"></SPAN>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" class=MsoNormal><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Verdana','sans-serif'; FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>

<P><STRONG>Transfers</STRONG></P></FONT>
<B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P>Nature of work - Retail/Wholesale</P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Description of processing</P></B>
<P>The following is a broad description of the way this organisation/data controller processes personal information. To understand how your own personal information is processed you may need to refer to any personal communications you have received, check any privacy notices the organisation has provided or contact the organisation to ask about your personal circumstances. </P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Reasons/purposes for processing information</P></B>
<P>We process personal information to enable us to buy, sell, promote and advertise our products and services; maintain our own accounts and records; support and manage our employees; the trading and sharing of personal information; the use of CCTV systems for crime prevention.</P>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>family details 
<LI>lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>education and employment details 
<LI>financial details 
<LI>goods and services</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include: </P>
<UL>
<LI>racial or ethnic origin 
<LI>religious or other beliefs 
<LI>trade union membership 
<LI>physical or mental health details 
<LI>offences and alleged offences 
<LI>visual images, personal appearance and behaviour 
<LI>criminal proceedings and behaviour</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about: </P>
<UL>
<LI>employees 
<LI>customers 
<LI>suppliers 
<LI>service providers 
<LI>enquirers, complainants 
<LI>offenders and suspected offenders 
<LI>individuals captured by CCTV images</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Transfers</P>
<P></B>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information may be transferred to countries or territories around the world. Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</P></FONT>

<P>Personal information is also processed in order to undertake research. The sensitive types of information may include physical or mental health details, racial or ethnic origin and religious or other beliefs.</P>
<P>This information is about survey respondents. Where necessary or required this information may be shared with customers and clients, agents, service providers, survey and research organisations.</P>

<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>CCTV - Crime Prevention and/or Staff Monitoring </B></P>
<P>CCTV is used for maintaining the security of property and premises and for preventing and investigating crime, it may also be used to monitor staff when carrying out work duties. For these reasons the information processed may include visual images, personal appearance and behaviours. This information may be about staff, customers and clients, offenders and suspected offenders, members of the public and those inside, entering or in the immediate vicinity of the area under surveillance. Where necessary or required this information is shared with the data subjects themselves, employees and agents, services providers, police forces, security organisations and persons making an enquiry.</P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>

<P>Type/classes of information processed</P></B>
<P>We process information relevant to the above reasons/purposes. This information may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>personal details 
<LI>family details 
<LI>lifestyle and social circumstances 
<LI>goods and services 
<LI>financial details 
<LI>employment and education details </LI></UL>
<P><BR></P>
<P>We also process sensitive classes of information that may include:</P>
<UL>
<LI>physical or mental health details 
<LI>sexual life 
<LI>racial or ethnic origin 
<LI>trade union membership 
<LI>religious or other beliefs of a similar nature 
<LI>offences and alleged offences </LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information is processed about</P></B>
<P>We process personal information about our:</P>
<UL>
<LI>patients 
<LI>customers and clients 
<LI>staff 
<LI>suppliers 
<LI>business contacts 
<LI>professional advisers</LI></UL>
<P><BR></P><B>
<P>Who the information may be shared with</P></B>
<P>We sometimes need to share the personal information we process with the individual themself and also with other organisations. Where this is necessary we are required to comply with all aspects of the Data Protection Act (DPA). What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Where necessary or required we share information with:</P>
<UL>
<LI>healthcare professionals 
<LI>social and welfare organisations 
<LI>central government 
<LI>business associates 
<LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing 
<LI>suppliers and service providers; 
<LI>financial organisations 
<LI>current, past and prospective employers; 
<LI>employment agencies and examining bodies</LI></UL></FONT>
<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>CCTV - Crime Prevention and/or Staff Monitoring </B></P>
<P>CCTV is used for maintaining the security of property and premises and for preventing and investigating crime, it may also be used to monitor staff when carrying out work duties. For these reasons the information processed may include visual images, personal appearance and behaviours. This information may be about staff, customers and clients, offenders and suspected offenders, members of the public and those inside, entering or in the immediate vicinity of the area under surveillance. Where necessary or required this information is shared with the data subjects themselves, employees and agents, services providers, police forces, security organisations and persons making an enquiry.</P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>

<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>CCTV - Crime Prevention and/or Staff Monitoring </B></P>
<P>CCTV is used for maintaining the security of property and premises and for preventing and investigating crime, it may also be used to monitor staff when carrying out work duties. For these reasons the information processed may include visual images, personal appearance and behaviours. This information may be about staff, customers and clients, offenders and suspected offenders, members of the public and those inside, entering or in the immediate vicinity of the area under surveillance. Where necessary or required this information is shared with the data subjects themselves, employees and agents, services providers, police forces, security organisations and persons making an enquiry.</P></FONT>
<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>Undertaking Research </P></B>
<P>Personal information is also processed in order to undertake research. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, lifestyle and social circumstances, financial details, good and services. The sensitive types of information may include physical or mental health details, racial or ethnic origin and religious or other beliefs. This information is about survey respondents. Where necessary or required this information may be shared with customers and clients, agents, service providers, survey and research organisations.</P></FONT>
<P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>Trading and Sharing Personal Information</B></P>
<P>Personal information is traded and shared as a primary business function. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, financial details, employment details, and goods and services. This information may be about customers and clients. The information may be traded or shared with business associates and professional advisers, agents, service providers, customers and clients, voluntary and charitable organisations&nbsp;and traders in personal data.</P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Transfers</P>
<P></B>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information may be transferred to countries or territories around the world. Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</P>

<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 10pt" class=MsoNormal><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><FONT size=3><FONT face=Calibri>Queen’s Baton Relay<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></B></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 10pt" class=MsoNormal><FONT size=3><FONT face=Calibri>Personal information is also processed in order to stage the Queen’s Baton Relay which takes place prior to the Glasgow 2014 Commonwealth Games. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details and lifestyle and social circumstances. The sensitive types of information may include information about offences and criminal proceedings. This information is about baton bearer applicants, their nominators and relatives, guardians and associates of the baton bearer applicants. Where necessary or required this information may be shared with agents, service providers, sponsors, police forces, central and local government and security organisations.<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 10pt" class=MsoNormal><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><FONT size=3><FONT face=Calibri>Authorisation of advertising and trading activity<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></B></P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 10pt" class=MsoNormal><FONT size=3><FONT face=Calibri>Personal information is also processed in order to administer applications for advertising and trading at venues hosting the Glasgow 2014 Commonwealth Games pursuant to the Glasgow Commonwealth Games (Trading and Advertising) Regulations 2013. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details and social circumstances. This information is about<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>applicants and associates of applicants. <P>CCTV - Crime Prevention and/or Staff Monitoring </B></P>
<P>CCTV is used for maintaining the security of property and premises and for preventing and investigating crime, it may also be used to monitor staff when carrying out work duties. What follows is a description of the types of organisations we may need to share some of the personal information we process with for one or more reasons. </P><P><Br></P> <P>Where necessary or required we share information with: </P> <UL> <LI>family, associates and representatives of the person whose personal data we are processing</LI> <LI>healthcare, social and welfare advisers or practitioners</LI> <LI>business associates</LI> <LI>financial organisations and professional advisers</LI> <LI>credit reference agencies, debt collection and tracing agencies</LI> <LI>education, educators and examining bodies</LI> <LI>current, past or prospective employers</LI> <LI>employment and recruitment agencies</LI> <LI>schools</LI> <LI>local and central government</LI> <LI>persons making an enquiry or complaint</LI> <LI>suppliers</LI> <LI>service providers</LI></UL></FONT><P><BR></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B>
<P>CCTV - Crime Prevention and/or Staff Monitoring </B></P>
<P>CCTV is used for maintaining the security of property and premises and for preventing and investigating crime, it may also be used to monitor staff when carrying out work duties. For these reasons the information processed may include visual images, personal appearance and behaviours. This information may be about staff, customers and clients, offenders and suspected offenders, members of the public and those inside, entering or in the immediate vicinity of the area under surveillance. Where necessary or required this information is shared with the data subjects themselves, employees and agents, services providers, police forces, security organisations and persons making an enquiry.</P></FONT><P><Br></P><FONT size=2 face=verdana><B> <P>Undertaking Research </P></B><P>Personal information is also processed in order to undertake research. For this reason the information processed may include name, contact details, family details, lifestyle and social circumstances, financial details, good and services. The sensitive types of information may include physical or mental health details, racial or ethnic origin and religious or other beliefs. This information is about survey respondents. Where necessary or required this information may be shared with customers and clients, agents, service providers, survey and research organisations.</P></FONT><B><FONT size=2 face=verdana>
<P><BR></P>
<P>Transfers</P>
<P></B>It may sometimes be necessary to transfer personal information overseas. When this is needed information may be transferred to countries or territories around the world. Any transfers made will be in full compliance with all aspects of the data protection act.</P></FONT>
